	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != 'f3e7272a73e459ded23a89a1a17edb3de59c8b3d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'f3e7272a73e459ded23a89a1a17edb3de59c8b3d') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '140d32355d098023a5d8c36bbc078c2ca79ff779') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'f3e7272a73e459ded23a89a1a17edb3de59c8b3d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') != 'c4c997987316cbd5d994050885b57f2faf51ef14') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'c4c997987316cbd5d994050885b57f2faf51ef14') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'cdffae677b65e7515744ed86aaab16cc5ad739b2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'c4c997987316cbd5d994050885b57f2faf51ef14') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php') != '4491fb604e1209d0612013e856db18bcb7144860') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php') !== '4491fb604e1209d0612013e856db18bcb7144860') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php') !== '49fbde706a5bcae4c80a1396f332c62dc8396471') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php') !== '4491fb604e1209d0612013e856db18bcb7144860') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/logger/200_windows_eventlog/OIDplusLoggerPluginWindowsEventLog.class.php');
